info:Guestroom (Double Bed) (Balcony)
info:Stayed in April 2024
info:Couples
info:3 Reviews
rating:5
posted:Posted May 7, 2024
msg:Its our 2nd time in Wuzhen, so we prefer staying a night is the best way or the only way for tourist to enjoy wonders of Wuzhen Watertown. 

This hotel is located inside the watertown so you have the privilege to roam till late and as early in the morning. 

Since its our first time staying in the hotel, we are not aware that the hotel has 2 entrances. We checked in at the common area, while our luggages will be transported to our designated hotels, since we only had a day to explore, without dropping to our hotel we go straight to the West part of Wuzhen water town. 

This time we almost finish the whole area, and we felt so amazed with bands singing inside restaurants, and it turned out so well. 

During the day, you can enjoy the old  stone alley. We stayed in East gate, one unit has 3 rooms, 1 on the 1st floor (which we had), while 2 more rooms upstairs. Ground floor has a common area for morning tea time. 

We choose the lower ground since it has balcony overlooking a part of the watertown. While for the room, definitely its expected to be old style, but its clean, with typical Chinese decor of 4 posts bed frame, which practically makes the room a bit crowded. 

Breakfast is typical buffet type, good taste. Servers are very efficient, since guests coming in continuously. They're so attentive as soon as you finished your food, they'll surely cleans your plate out. 

Overall, we did enjoy our stay.

When you take the tour bus, you will be asked for your hotel and room number, and you can sit there. At the hotel where you are located, your luggage can be carried with the car or checked separately to the hotel for free. After arriving at the hotel, collect the room card and apply for face recognition at the hotel front desk in the scenic area, so that you can enter and exit the scenic area without restrictions during the check-in time. There are 350 morning tea customers in the scenic area on a first-come, first-served basis. If you exceed the number, you can also pay by yourself. The morning tea guest project is only open to tourists staying in the scenic spot. It basically ends at nine o'clock and will take some time. Those who are not morning tea drinkers can also have breakfast in the hotel.

msg:When I came to Wuzhen for a trip, I chose Pillow Water Resort Hotel after careful consideration. It was really the best choice. The location is very good. There are battery cars in and out of the hotel, so there is no need to walk. It is suitable for taking the elderly to travel. The hotel has warm and thoughtful service, good hygiene, rest assured, and a wide variety of breakfasts. The surrounding environment is good, especially the quiet time in the morning and evening. I stayed for two nights and went out in the morning and evening. There are few people and beautiful scenery. I have a good impression of Wuzhen. It has a lot to do with the service and location of the hotel. Recommend pillow water. The downside is: the first floor is a bit damp, the price-performance ratio is not very high, not as good as the five-star hotel facilities at the same price.

msg:Wuzhen Xizha is a great scenic spot to relax. Zhenshui is a decent hotel in Xizha Scenic Area. This time I stayed in its homestay area. There are retail tenants in one building. We lived in two houses. The third one was noisy when the door was opened back and forth in the middle of the night. I can't sleep, sound insulation and design are not good. But after all, the requirements for an old house cannot be high. The facilities in the room are okay. The beds are characteristic and antique, the bathroom is a bit small and cramped, and the location is good. It is in the bustling Nvhong Street in the middle. The service is also very good. Dim sum is delivered every day, and the lobby manager still walks a long way (far between things and things) to help me find my luggage.
The breakfast is quite generous, the Chinese restaurant dinner is very good, the taste is good and the price is decent.
